name:hâ€râ€xâ€s
info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Other
info:2 Reviews
rating:1
posted:Posted October 21, 2021
msg:I came with full expectations, but left with disappointment. The security guards at Delta are as fierce as ***!
I still remember that the first time I came to Delta was to attend a friend's wedding. My first impression at that time was that our Baoshan hotels can also be high-end! Later, I bought some meal coupons to consume several times, and I liked the environment of the hotel very much. After that, I came to take pictures for the first time. The service staff of the hotel were very enthusiastic at that time. I stayed there several times afterwards, and I took a lot of photos every time I came. Because the hotel environment is good, I was very satisfied with the photos I took every time. (I would like to explain here that although I took a lot of photos, there were actually only two people taking pictures, one model and the other was me, and I took pictures with my mobile phone. We changed clothes in the room and went outside the hotel to take pictures. Back and forth, so many times, we always found places with few people outside the hotel to take pictures.)
This time I came to stay again, and found that many of the hotel service staff had changed, and the service was not as enthusiastic as before. There was an enterprise event and a wedding celebration that day, and the whole hotel was in chaos. As usual, I took the model to change clothes in the room and took photos outside the hotel downstairs. There were still two people and one mobile phone. I didn't expect that I was stopped by the security guard this time. The security guard was very fierce and said that we were not allowed to take photos. I said that we were guests and it was not the first time we came back. Why couldn't we take photos this time? The security guard said that I took too many photos and it was commercial in nature, so we couldn't take photos. I said that I had come here so many times and this was the first time you said that. Then I saw that many people were also taking photos in the lobby, and I didn't have any other equipment. I just took a mobile phone to take photos, and I didn't find any places with people. Then the security guard said: If you say that, I will call someone! Wearing a black suit, he looked so fierce. Forget it, you have the final say in your territory, I will stay away.
Finally, I want to express my personal feelings. The environment of the hotel is very beautiful and high-end. I hope the hotel's service can also be high-end. Be polite to guests and communicate well if there are any problems! Don't be so fierce!
